SELECT TO_CHAR(RPAD(NVL(yhzh, ' '), 20, ' '))||TO_CHAR(Rpad(substr(zhm , 1, 10), 10, ' '))||TO_CHAR(Rpad(substr(gh, 1, 10), 10, ' '))||TO_CHAR(Rpad('1', 10, ' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(NVL(sfzh, ' '), 20, ' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(sum(btje), 16, ' '), '999999999999.99')||TO_CHAR(substr(rpad('a', 21, ' '), 2, 20))   FROM  COUNTYDATA.rcbtdjtemp  WHERE FF=0 AND BTJE>0  and btlx ='0598' and batchid in (119)  group by gh,yhzh,zhm,sfzh order by yhzh,gh

SELECT A.REGID,B.OBJECTCODE,B.SSSSOBJECTNAME,B.HOMEADDRESS,A.TYPEID, D.TYPENAME,A.TYPECODE,A.REGMONEY FROM COUNTYDATA.FSREGISTRATION A LEFT JOIN V_BASEOBJECT B ON A.OBJECTID=B.OBJECTID  LEFT JOIN COUNTYDATA.FSTYPE D ON A.TYPECODE=D.TYPECODE WHERE A.REGMONEY>0 AND SUBSTR(B.OBJECTCODE,1,9)=SUBSTR(D.CATEGORYCODE,1,9) AND LENGTH(D.CATEGORYCODE)=9  AND A.FSYEAR=2015 AND A.TYPECODE='0542' AND A.LSSUECYCLE=3 AND A.OFFSET='02' ORDER BY B.OBJECTCODE

SELECT A.REGID,B.OBJECTCODE,B.SSSSOBJECTNAME,B.HOMEADDRESS,A.TYPEID, D.TYPENAME,A.TYPECODE,A.REGMONEY FROM COUNTYDATA.FSREGISTRATION A LEFT JOIN V_BASEOBJECT B ON A.OBJECTID=B.OBJECTID  LEFT JOIN COUNTYDATA.FSTYPE D ON A.TYPECODE=D.TYPECODE WHERE A.REGMONEY>0 AND SUBSTR(B.OBJECTCODE,1,9)=SUBSTR(D.CATEGORYCODE,1,9) AND LENGTH(D.CATEGORYCODE)=9  AND A.FSYEAR=2015 AND A.TYPECODE='0542' AND A.LSSUECYCLE=3 AND A.OFFSET='02' ORDER BY B.OBJECTCODE

SELECT A.OBJECTCODE,A.ACCOUNTNUM,A.SSSSOBJECTNAME,d.GH,A.SSSSIDCARDNUM,SUM(C.REGMONEY) FROM V_BASEOBJECT A INNER JOIN COUNTYDATA.FSREGISTRATION C ON A.OBJECTID=C.OBJECTID  INNER JOIN COUNTYDATA.OBJECTGH D ON A.OBJECTID=D.ID  WHERE a.isenable=1 and c.REGMONEY>0  and c.iseffect=0 AND C.TYPECODE IN (0223) AND C.FSYEAR=2015 AND C.BANKCODE='001' group by A.OBJECTCODE,A.ACCOUNTNUM,a.SSSSOBJECTNAME,d.GH,a.SSSSIDCARDNUM order by A.ACCOUNTNUM DESC,d.GH
SELECT TO_CHAR(RPAD(NVL(ACCOUNTNUM,' '),20,' '))||TO_CHAR(Rpad(substr(SSSSOBJECTNAME, 1, 10), 10, ' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(substr(GH,1,10),10,' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD('1',10,' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(NVL(SSSSIDCARDNUM, ' '), 20, ' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(sum(REGMONEY),16,' '),'999999999999.99')||TO_CHAR(substr(rpad('a',21,' '),2,22))  FROM COUNTYDATA.CURRENTPAY  group by gh,ACCOUNTNUM,SSSSOBJECTNAME,SSSSIDCARDNUM order by accountnum
SELECT A.OBJECTCODE,A.ACCOUNTNUM,A.SSSSOBJECTNAME,d.GH,A.SSSSIDCARDNUM,SUM(C.REGMONEY) FROM V_BASEOBJECT A INNER JOIN COUNTYDATA.FSREGISTRATION C ON A.OBJECTID=C.OBJECTID  INNER JOIN COUNTYDATA.OBJECTGH D ON A.OBJECTID=D.ID  WHERE a.isenable=1 and c.REGMONEY>0  and c.iseffect=0 AND C.TYPECODE IN (0234) AND C.FSYEAR=2015 AND C.BANKCODE='001' group by A.OBJECTCODE,A.ACCOUNTNUM,a.SSSSOBJECTNAME,d.GH,a.SSSSIDCARDNUM order by A.ACCOUNTNUM DESC,d.GH
SELECT TO_CHAR(RPAD(NVL(ACCOUNTNUM,' '),20,' '))||TO_CHAR(Rpad(substr(SSSSOBJECTNAME, 1, 10), 10, ' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(substr(GH,1,10),10,' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD('1',10,' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(NVL(SSSSIDCARDNUM, ' '), 20, ' '))||TO_CHAR(RPAD(sum(REGMONEY),16,' '),'999999999999.99')||TO_CHAR(substr(rpad('a',21,' '),2,22))  FROM COUNTYDATA.CURRENTPAY  group by gh,ACCOUNTNUM,SSSSOBJECTNAME,SSSSIDCARDNUM order by accountnum

SELECT a.dz,a.gh,a.object_name,a.zhm,a.lxdh,a.sfzh,a.yhzh,c.TYPENAME,a.btsl,a.btbz,a.btje,a.ff,a.ffdate,a.wfyy,b.batchname FROM   COUNTYDATA.rcbtdjtemp a,COUNTYDATA.batch b,COUNTYDATA.FSTYPE c where a.batchid=b.batchid and a.btlx=c.typecode  and ff=0  and a.batchid='94'  and a.btlx='0599'   group by gh,dz,object_name,zhm,lxdh,sfzh,yhzh,typename,btsl,btbz,btje,ff,ffdate,wfyy,batchname order by gh
